         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Data loading helper functions
         
         def load_restaurants():
             restaurants = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'restaurant.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         restaurants[parts[0]] = {
                             'restaurant_id': parts[0],
                             'name': parts[1],
                             'cuisine': parts[2],
                             'address': parts[3],
                             'phone': parts[4],
                             'rating': parts[5],
                             'delivery_time': parts[6],
                             'min_order': parts[7]
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return restaurants
         
         
         def load_menus():
             menus = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'menu.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         menus[parts[0]] = {
                             'item_id': parts[0],
                             'restaurant_id': parts[1],
                             'item_name': parts[2],
                             'category': parts[3],
                             'description': parts[4],
                             'price': parts[5],
                             'availability': parts[6]
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return menus
         
         
         def load_cart():
             cart = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'cart.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         cart[parts[0]] = {
                             'cart_id': parts[0],
                             'item_id': parts[1],
                             'restaurant_id': parts[2],
                             'quantity': parts[3],
                             'added_date': parts[4]
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return cart
         
         
         def load_orders():
             orders = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'order.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) < 8:
                             continue
                         order_id = parts[0]
                         customer_name = parts[1]
                         restaurant_id = parts[2]
                         order_date = parts[3]
                         total_amount = parts[4]
                         status = parts[5]
                         delivery_address = ','.join(parts[6:-1])
                         phone_number = parts[-1]
                         try:
                             status_int = int(status)
                         except Exception:
                             status_int = 0
                         orders[order_id] = {
                             'order_id': order_id,
                             'customer_name': customer_name,
                             'restaurant_id': restaurant_id,
                             'order_date': order_date,
                             'total_amount': total_amount,
                             'status': status_int,
                             'delivery_address': delivery_address,
                             'phone_number': phone_number
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return orders
         
         
         def load_order_items():
             order_items = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'order_items.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         order_item_id, order_id, item_id, quantity, price = parts
                         if order_id not in order_items:
                             order_items[order_id] = []
                         order_items[order_id].append({
                             'order_item_id': order_item_id,
                             'item_id': item_id,
                             'quantity': quantity,
                             'price': price
                         })
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return order_items
         
         
         def load_deliveries():
             deliveries = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'delivery.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         delivery_id, order_id, driver_name, driver_phone, vehicle_info, status, estimated_time = parts
                         deliveries[order_id] = {
                             'delivery_id': delivery_id,
                             'driver_name': driver_name,
                             'driver_phone': driver_phone,
                             'vehicle_info': vehicle_info,
                             'status': status,
                             'estimated_time': estimated_time
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return deliveries
         
         
         def load_reviews():
             reviews = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'review.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) < 6:
                             continue
                         review_id, restaurant_id, customer_name, rating = parts[0:4]
                         review_text = ','.join(parts[4:-1])
                         review_date = parts[-1]
                         if restaurant_id not in reviews:
                             reviews[restaurant_id] = []
                         reviews[restaurant_id].append({
                             'review_id': review_id,
                             'customer_name': customer_name,
                             'rating': rating,
                             'review_text': review_text,
                             'review_date': review_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return reviews
         
         
         # Routes
         
         @app.route('/', methods=['POST'])
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard', methods=['POST'])
         def dashboard():
             restaurants = load_restaurants()
             try:
                 featured_restaurants = sorted(restaurants.values(), key=lambda r: float(r['rating']), reverse=True)[:3]
             except Exception:
                 featured_restaurants = list(restaurants.values())[:3]
         
             cuisine_count = {}
             for r in restaurants.values():
                 cuisine_count[r['cuisine']] = cuisine_count.get(r['cuisine'], 0) + 1
             popular_cuisine = max(cuisine_count, key=cuisine_count.get) if cuisine_count else ''
         
             return render_template('dashboard.htm', featured_restaurants=featured_restaurants, popular_cuisine=popular_cuisine)
         
         
         @app.route('/restaurants', methods=['POST'])
         def browse_restaurants():
             restaurants = load_restaurants()
             cuisines = {}
             for r in restaurants.values():
                 cuisines.setdefault(r['cuisine'], []).append(r)
         
             search_query_raw = request.form.get('search_query', '')
             search_query = [s.strip().lower() for s in search_query_raw.split()] if search_query_raw else []
         
             if search_query:
                 filtered_restaurants = []
                 for r in restaurants.values():
                     text = (r['name'] + ' ' + r['cuisine'] + ' ' + r['address']).lower()
                     if all(term in text for term in search_query):
                         filtered_restaurants.append(r)
             else:
                 filtered_restaurants = list(restaurants.values())
         
             return render_template('restaurants.html', restaurants=filtered_restaurants, cuisines=cuisines, search_query=search_query)
         
         
         @app.route('/menu/<int:restaurant_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def restaurant_menu(restaurant_id):
             restaurants = load_restaurants()
             menus = load_menus()
         
             restaurant = next((r for r in restaurants.values() if int(r['restaurant_id']) == restaurant_id), None)
             if not restaurant:
                 return "Restaurant not found", 404
         
             menu_items = [m for m in menus.values() if m['restaurant_id'] == str(restaurant_id) and m['availability'] == '1']
         
             menu_item = menu_items[0] if menu_items else {}
         
             return render_template('menu.html', restaurant=restaurant, menu_item=menu_item, restaurant_id=restaurant_id)
         
         
         @app.route('/item/<int:item_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def item_details(item_id):
             menus = load_menus()
         
             item = next((m for m in menus.values() if int(m['item_id']) == item_id), None)
             if not item:
                 return "Item not found", 404
         
             return render_template('item_detail.html', item=item, item=item_id)
         
         
         @app.route('/cart', methods=['GET'])
         def shopping_cart():
             cart = load_cart()
             menus = load_menus()
         
             cart_items = {}
             total_amount = 0.0
         
             for c in cart.values():
                 item_id = c['item_id']
                 quantity = 0
                 try:
                     quantity = int(c['quantity'])
                 except Exception:
                     quantity = 0
         
                 item = menus.get(item_id)
                 if not item:
                     continue
         
                 try:
                     price = float(item['price'])
                 except Exception:
                     price = 0.0
         
                 total_price = price * quantity
         
                 cart_items[item_id] = {
                     'item': item,
                     'quantity': quantity,
                     'total_price': total_price
                 }
                 total_amount += total_price
         
             total_amount = int(total_amount)  # as per spec, total_amount as integer
         
             return render_template('cart.htm', cart_items=cart_items, total_amount=total_amount)
         
         
         @app.route('/checkout', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def checkout():
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 delivery_info = [
                     request.form.get('customer_name', ''),
                     request.form.get('delivery_address', ''),
                     request.form.get('phone_number', ''),
                     request.form.get('payment_method', '')
                 ]
                 return render_template('checkout.html', delivery_info=delivery_info)
             else:
                 cart = load_cart()
                 menus = load_menus()
                 cart_items = {}
                 for c in cart.values():
                     item_id = c['item_id']
                     quantity = 0
                     try:
                         quantity = int(c['quantity'])
                     except Exception:
                         quantity = 0
                     item = menus.get(item_id)
                     if not item:
                         continue
                     cart_items[item_id] = {
                         'item': item,
                         'quantity': quantity
                     }
                 return render_template('checkout.html', cart_items=cart_items)
         
         
         @app.route('/orders/active', methods=['POST'])
         def active_orders():
             orders = load_orders()
             status_filter_str = request.form.get('status_filter', '0')
             try:
                 status_filter = int(status_filter_str)
             except Exception:
                 status_filter = 0
         
             if status_filter == 0:
                 filtered_orders = orders
             else:
                 filtered_orders = {oid: o for oid, o in orders.items() if o['status'] == status_filter}
         
             return render_template('active_orders.html', active_orders=filtered_orders, status_filter=status_filter)
         
         
         @app.route('/orders/track/<int:order_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def order_tracking(order_id):
             orders = load_orders()
             deliveries = load_deliveries()
             order_items = load_order_items()
             menus = load_menus()
         
             order = next((o for o in orders.values() if int(o['order_id']) == order_id), None)
             if not order:
                 return "Order not found", 404
         
             delivery_driver = deliveries.get(str(order_id), [])
             items_for_order = order_items.get(str(order_id), [])
         
             detailed_order_items = {}
             for item in items_for_order:
                 item_id = item['item_id']
                 quantity = item['quantity']
                 price = item['price']
                 item_detail = menus.get(item_id)
                 if item_detail:
                     detailed_order_items[item_id] = {
                         'item': item_detail,
                         'quantity': quantity,
                         'price': price
                     }
         
             return render_template('track_order.html', order=order, delivery_driver=delivery_driver, order_items=detailed_order_items, order=order_id)
         
         
         @app.route('/reviews', methods=['POST'])
         def reviews():
             all_reviews = load_reviews()
             filter_rating_str = request.form.get('filter_rating', '0')
             try:
                 filter_rating = int(filter_rating_str)
             except Exception:
                 filter_rating = 0
         
             if filter_rating == 0:
                 filtered_reviews = all_reviews
             else:
                 filtered_reviews = {}
                 for rid, rev_list in all_reviews.items():
                     filtered_list = [r for r in rev_list if int(r['rating']) == filter_rating]
                     if filtered_list:
                         filtered_reviews[rid] = filtered_list
         
             return render_template('reviews_html', reviews=filtered_reviews, filter_rating=filter_rating)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

      📄 Before (full content):
         # FoodDelivery Web Application Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         | Route Path                  | Function Name         | HTTP Method | Template File          | Context Variables (name:type)                                        | Dynamic Parameters                 |
         |-----------------------------|-----------------------|-------------|------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|
         | /                           | root_redirect          | GET         | N/A (redirect)          | N/A                                                                 | N/A                              |
         | /dashboard                  | dashboard             | GET         | dashboard.html          | featured_restaurants: List[dict], popular_cuisines: List[str]         | N/A                              |
         | /restaurants                | browse_restaurants    | GET         | restaurants.html        | restaurants: List[dict], cuisines: List[str], search_query: str        | N/A                              |
         | /menu/<int:restaurant_id>   | restaurant_menu       | GET         | menu.html               | restaurant: dict, menu_items: List[dict]                             | restaurant_id:int                 |
         | /item/<int:item_id>         | item_details          | GET         | item_details.html       | item: dict                                                          | item_id:int                      |
         | /cart                      | shopping_cart         | GET, POST    | cart.html               | cart_items: List[dict], total_amount: float                         | N/A                              |
         | /checkout                  | checkout              | GET, POST    | checkout.html           | cart_items: List[dict] (GET), delivery_info: dict (POST)             | N/A                              |
         | /orders/active             | active_orders         | GET         | active_orders.html      | active_orders: List[dict], status_filter: str                       | N/A                              |
         | /orders/track/<int:order_id>| order_tracking        | GET         | track_order.html        | order: dict, delivery_driver: dict, order_items: List[dict]          | order_id:int                    |
         | /reviews                   | reviews               | GET         | reviews.html            | reviews: List[dict], filter_rating: str                             | N/A                              |
         
         Notes:
         - The root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
         - POST methods on `/cart` route allow updating cart quantities/removal.
         - POST method on `/checkout` allows submitting delivery and payment info to place order.
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications
         
         ### 1. dashboard.html
         - File Path: templates/dashboard.html
         - Page Title: Food Delivery Dashboard
         - Layout: Main dashboard container with featured restaurants, popular cuisines, and navigation buttons.
         - Element IDs and Types:
           - dashboard-page (div)
           - featured-restaurants (div)
           - browse-restaurants-button (button)
           - view-cart-button (button)
           - active-orders-button (button)
         - Navigation Mapping:
           - browse-restaurants-button => browse_restaurants (url_for)
           - view-cart-button => shopping_cart
           - active-orders-button => active_orders
         
         ---
         
         ### 2. restaurants.html
         - File Path: templates/restaurants.html
         - Page Title: Browse Restaurants
         - Layout: Search/filter bar on top, grid of restaurant cards below.
         - Element IDs:
           - restaurants-page (div)
           - search-input (input)
           - cuisine-filter (select/dropdown)
           - restaurants-grid (div)
           - view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id} (button) for each restaurant card
         - Navigation:
           - view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id} => restaurant_menu with restaurant_id parameter
         
         ---
         
         ### 3. menu.html
         - File Path: templates/menu.html
         - Page Title: Restaurant Menu
         - Layout: Header with restaurant name and info, grid of menu items.
         - Element IDs:
           - menu-page (div)
           - restaurant-name (h1)
           - restaurant-info (div)
           - menu-items-grid (div)
           - add-to-cart-button-{item_id} (button) per menu item
           - view-item-details-{item_id} (button) per menu item
         - Navigation:
           - view-item-details-{item_id} => item_details with item_id
         
         ---
         
         ### 4. item_details.html
         - File Path: templates/item_details.html
         - Page Title: Item Details
         - Layout: Item detail container with name, description, price and quantity input.
         - Element IDs:
           - item-details-page (div)
           - item-name (h1)
           - item-description (div)
           - item-price (div)
           - quantity-input (input number)
           - add-to-cart-button (button)
         
         ---
         
         ### 5. cart.html
         - File Path: templates/cart.html
         - Page Title: Shopping Cart
         - Layout: Container with table listing cart items, update quantity inputs and remove buttons, total amount, and proceed button.
         - Element IDs:
           - cart-page (div)
           - cart-items-table (table)
           - update-quantity-{item_id} (input number) per cart item
           - remove-item-button-{item_id} (button) per cart item
           - proceed-checkout-button (button)
           - total-amount (div)
         
         ---
         
         ### 6. checkout.html
         - File Path: templates/checkout.html
         - Page Title: Checkout
         - Layout: Form with fields for customer name, address, phone, payment method, and place order button.
         - Element IDs:
           - checkout-page (div)
           - customer-name (input)
           - delivery-address (textarea)
           - phone-number (input)
           - payment-method (select/dropdown)
           - place-order-button (button)
         
         ---
         
         ### 7. active_orders.html
         - File Path: templates/active_orders.html
         - Page Title: Active Orders
         - Layout: List of orders with a filter dropdown and navigation buttons.
         - Element IDs:
           - active-orders-page (div)
           - orders-list (div)
           - track-order-button-{order_id} (button) per order
           - status-filter (select/dropdown)
           - back-to-dashboard (button)
         - Navigation:
           - back-to-dashboard => dashboard
           - track-order-button-{order_id} => order_tracking with order_id
         
         ---
         
         ### 8. track_order.html
         - File Path: templates/track_order.html
         - Page Title: Track Order
         - Layout: Detailed order tracking container with delivery driver info and back button.
         - Element IDs:
           - tracking-page (div)
           - order-details (div)
           - delivery-driver-info (div)
           - estimated-time (div)
           - order-items-list (div)
           - back-to-orders (button)
         - Navigation:
           - back-to-orders => active_orders
         
         ---
         
         ### 9. reviews.html
         - File Path: templates/reviews.html
         - Page Title: Order Reviews
         - Layout: List of reviews with filter dropdown and navigation buttons.
         - Element IDs:
           - reviews-page (div)
           - reviews-list (div)
           - write-review-button (button)
           - filter-by-rating (select/dropdown)
           - back-to-dashboard (button)
         - Navigation:
           - write-review-button (button) [Note: navigation to a write review feature not detailed]
           - back-to-dashboard => dashboard
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data Schemas
         
         ### 1. restaurants.txt
         - File: data/restaurants.txt
         - Fields (order and pipe-separated):
           restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order
         - Purpose: Stores restaurant details including contact, cuisine, rating, and delivery parameters.
         - Data Types:
           - restaurant_id: int
           - name: string
           - cuisine: string
           - address: string
           - phone: string
           - rating: float
           - delivery_time: int (minutes)
           - min_order: float
         - Examples:
           1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00
           2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00
           3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00
         
         ---
         
         ### 2. menus.txt
         - File: data/menus.txt
         - Fields:
           item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability
         - Purpose: Contains all menu items linked to restaurants with descriptions and availability.
         - Data Types:
           - item_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - item_name: string
           - category: string
           - description: string
           - price: float
           - availability: int (0 or 1)
         - Examples:
           1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1
           2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1
           3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1
         
         ---
         
         ### 3. cart.txt
         - File: data/cart.txt
         - Fields:
           cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date
         - Purpose: Stores items currently in the shopping cart with quantity and date added.
         - Data Types:
           - cart_id: int
           - item_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - quantity: int
           - added_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Examples:
           1|1|1|2|2025-01-15
           2|3|2|1|2025-01-16
         
         ---
         
         ### 4. orders.txt
         - File: data/orders.txt
         - Fields:
           order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number
         - Purpose: Stores placed orders and tracking status.
         - Data Types:
           - order_id: int
           - customer_name: string
           - restaurant_id: int
           - order_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
           - total_amount: float
           - status: string (e.g., Delivered, On the Way)
           - delivery_address: string
           - phone_number: string
         - Examples:
           1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234
           2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678
         
         ---
         
         ### 5. order_items.txt
         - File: data/order_items.txt
         - Fields:
           order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price
         - Purpose: Detailed items belonging to each order.
         - Data Types:
           - order_item_id: int
           - order_id: int
           - item_id: int
           - quantity: int
           - price: float
         - Examples:
           1|1|1|2|12.99
           2|1|2|1|8.99
           3|2|3|1|14.99
         
         ---
         
         ### 6. deliveries.txt
         - File: data/deliveries.txt
         - Fields:
           delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time
         - Purpose: Stores delivery and driver assignment and tracking.
         - Data Types:
           - delivery_id: int
           - order_id: int
           - driver_name: string
           - driver_phone: string
           - vehicle_info: string
           - status: string
           - estimated_time: datetime (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         - Examples:
           1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45
           2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30
         
         ---
         
         ### 7. reviews.txt
         - File: data/reviews.txt
         - Fields:
           review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date
         - Purpose: Stores customer reviews for restaurants.
         - Data Types:
           - review_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - customer_name: string
           - rating: int (1-5)
           - review_text: string
           - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Examples:
           1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12
           2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13
           3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15
         
         ---
         
         # End of Design Specification

         ## Section 3: Data Schemas
         
         ### 1. restaurants.txt
         - File: data/restaurants.txt
         - Fields (order and pipe-separated):
           restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order
         - Purpose: Stores restaurant details including contact
          cuisine
          rating
          and delivery parameters.
         - Data Types:
           - restaurant_id: int
           - name: string
           - cuisine: string
           - address: string
           - phone: string
           - rating: float
           - delivery_time: int (minutes)
           - min_order: float
         - Examples:
           1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00
           2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00
           3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00
         
         ---
         
         ### 2. menus.txt
         - File: data/menus.txt
         - Fields:
           item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability
         - Purpose: Contains all menu items linked to restaurants with descriptions and availability.
         - Data Types:
           - item_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - item_name: string
           - category: string
           - description: string
           - price: float
           - availability: int (0 or 1)
         - Examples:
           1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1
           2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1
           3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1
         
         ---
         
         ### 3. cart.txt
         - File: data/cart.txt
         - Fields:
           cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date
         - Purpose: Stores items currently in the shopping cart with quantity and date added.
         - Data Types:
           - cart_id: int
           - item_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - quantity: int
           - added_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Examples:
           1|1|1|2|2025-01-15
           2|3|2|1|2025-01-16
         
         ---
         
         ### 4. orders.txt
         - File: data/orders.txt
         - Fields:
           order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number
         - Purpose: Stores placed orders and tracking status.
         - Data Types:
           - order_id: int
           - customer_name: string
           - restaurant_id: int
           - order_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
           - total_amount: float
           - status: string (e.g.
          Delivered
          On the Way)
           - delivery_address: string
           - phone_number: string
         - Examples:
           1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St
          NYC|555-1234
           2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave
          LA|555-5678
         
         ---
         
         ### 5. order_items.txt
         - File: data/order_items.txt
         - Fields:
           order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price
         - Purpose: Detailed items belonging to each order.
         - Data Types:
           - order_item_id: int
           - order_id: int
           - item_id: int
           - quantity: int
           - price: float
         - Examples:
           1|1|1|2|12.99
           2|1|2|1|8.99
           3|2|3|1|14.99
         
         ---
         
         ### 6. deliveries.txt
         - File: data/deliveries.txt
         - Fields:
           delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time
         - Purpose: Stores delivery and driver assignment and tracking.
         - Data Types:
           - delivery_id: int
           - order_id: int
           - driver_name: string
           - driver_phone: string
           - vehicle_info: string
           - status: string
           - estimated_time: datetime (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         - Examples:
           1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45
           2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30
         
         ---
         
         ### 7. reviews.txt
         - File: data/reviews.txt
         - Fields:
           review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date
         - Purpose: Stores customer reviews for restaurants.
         - Data Types:
           - review_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - customer_name: string
           - rating: int (1-5)
           - review_text: string
           - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Examples:
           1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12
           2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta
          slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13

         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         | Route Path                  | Function Name         | HTTP Method | Template File          | Context Variables (name:type)                                        | Dynamic Parameters                 |
         |-----------------------------|-----------------------|-------------|------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|
         | /                           | root_redirect          | GET         | N/A (redirect to /dashboard) | N/A                                                                 | N/A                              |
         | /dashboard                  | dashboard             | GET         | dashboard.html          | featured_restaurants: List[dict], popular_cuisines: List[str]         | N/A                              |
         | /restaurants                | browse_restaurants    | GET         | restaurants.html        | restaurants: List[dict], cuisines: List[str], search_query: str        | N/A                              |
         | /menu/<int:restaurant_id>   | restaurant_menu       | GET         | menu.html               | restaurant: dict, menu_items: List[dict]                             | restaurant_id:int                 |
         | /item/<int:item_id>         | item_details          | GET         | item_details.html       | item: dict                                                          | item_id:int                      |
         | /cart                      | shopping_cart         | GET, POST    | cart.html               | cart_items: List[dict], total_amount: float                         | N/A                              |
         | /checkout                  | checkout              | GET, POST    | checkout.html           | delivery_info: dict (POST), cart_items: List[dict] (GET)             | N/A                              |
         | /orders/active             | active_orders         | GET         | active_orders.html      | active_orders: List[dict], status_filter: str                       | N/A                              |
         | /orders/track/<int:order_id>| order_tracking        | GET         | track_order.html        | order: dict, delivery_driver: dict, order_items: List[dict]          | order_id:int                    |
         | /reviews                   | reviews               | GET         | reviews.html            | reviews: List[dict], filter_rating: str                             | N/A                              |

         - Navigation:
           - view-item-details-{item_id} triggers url_for('item_detail'
          item_id=itemid)

         ## Section 3: Data Schemas
         
         ### 1. restaurants.txt
         - File: data/restaurant.txt
         - Fields (comma-separated):
           restaurant_id,name,cuisine,address,phone,rating,delivery_time,min_order
         - Purpose: Store restaurant details including contact info
          cuisines
          rating
          delivery times
          and minimum order amounts.
         - Data Types:
           - restaurant_id: string
           - name: int
           - cuisine: int
           - address: int
           - phone: int
           - rating: string
           - delivery_time: string (minutes)
           - min_order: int
         - Example Data:
           1,Dragon House,Chinese,123 Main St,555-0001,4.5,30,15.00
           2,La Bella Italia,Italian,456 Oak Ave,555-0002,4.8,25,20.00
           3,Taj Mahal,Indian,789 Elm St,555-0003,4.6,35,18.00
         
         ---
         
         ### 2. menus.txt
         - File: data/menu.txt
         - Fields:
           item_id,restaurant_id,item_name,category,description,price,availability
         - Purpose: Contains menu items with details and availability status
         - Data Types:
           - item_id: string
           - restaurant_id: string
           - item_name: int
           - category: int
           - description: int
           - price: string
           - availability: string (0 or 1)
         - Example Data:
           1,1,Fried Rice,Main Course,Steamed rice with vegetables and egg,12.99,1
           2,1,Spring Rolls,Appetizer,Crispy rolls with pork filling,8.99,1
           3,2,Spaghetti Carbonara,Pasta,Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce,14.99,1
         
         ---
         
         ### 3. cart.txt
         - File: data/cart.txt
         - Fields:
           cart_id,item_id,restaurant_id,quantity,added_date
         - Purpose: Stores current shopping cart items with quantities and addition dates
         - Data Types:
           - cart_id: string
           - item_id: string
           - restaurant_id: string
           - quantity: string
           - added_date: string (YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Example Data:
           1,1,1,2,2025-01-15
           2,3,2,1,2025-01-16
         
         ---
         
         ### 4. orders.txt
         - File: data/order.txt
         - Fields:
           order_id,customer_name,restaurant_id,order_date,total_amount,status,delivery_address,phone_number
         - Purpose: Store order information including status and contact details
         - Data Types:
           - order_id: string
           - customer_name: int
           - restaurant_id: string
           - order_date: string (YYYY-MM-DD)
           - total_amount: string
           - status: int
           - delivery_address: int
           - phone_number: int
         - Example Data:
           1,John Doe,1,2025-01-10,21.98,Delivered,123 Main St
          NYC,555-1234
           2,Jane Smith,2,2025-01-14,14.99,On the Way,456 Oak Ave
          LA,555-5678
         
         ---
         
         ### 5. order_items.txt
         - File: data/order_items.txt
         - Fields:
           order_item_id,order_id,item_id,quantity,price
         - Purpose: Lists items included in orders with purchase quantities and prices
         - Data Types:
           - order_item_id: string
           - order_id: string
           - item_id: string
           - quantity: string
           - price: string
         - Example Data:
           1,1,1,2,12.99
           2,1,2,1,8.99
           3,2,3,1,14.99
         
         ---
         
         ### 6. deliveries.txt
         - File: data/delivery.txt
         - Fields:
           delivery_id,order_id,driver_name,driver_phone,vehicle_info,status,estimated_time
         - Purpose: Stores delivery assignements and status details
         - Data Types:
           - delivery_id: string
           - order_id: string
           - driver_name: int
           - driver_phone: int
           - vehicle_info: int
           - status: int
           - estimated_time: string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         - Example Data:
           1,1,Mike Johnson,555-9001,Bike,Delivered,2025-01-10 18:45
           2,2,Sarah Williams,555-9002,Car,On the Way,2025-01-14 19:30
         
         ---
         
         ### 7. reviews.txt
         - File: data/review.txt
         - Fields:
           review_id,restaurant_id,customer_name,rating,review_text,review_date
         - Purpose: Holds customer reviews for restaurants
         - Data Types:
           - review_id: string
           - restaurant_id: string
           - customer_name: int
           - rating: string (1 to 5)
           - review_text: int
           - review_date: string (YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Example Data:
           1,1,Alice Johnson,5,Excellent food and fast delivery!,2025-01-12
           2,2,Bob Williams,4,Great pasta
          slightly delayed delivery.,2025-01-13
           3,3,Charlie Brown,5,Best Indian food in town!,2025-01-15
         
         ---

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         import os
         import datetime
         
         # Helper functions to load data from files
         
         def load_restaurants():
             restaurants = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'restaurant.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         restaurant_id = parts[0]
                         restaurants[restaurant_id] = {
                             'restaurant_id': parts[0],
                             'name': parts[1],
                             'cuisine': parts[2],
                             'address': parts[3],
                             'phone': parts[4],
                             'rating': parts[5],
                             'delivery_time': parts[6],
                             'min_order': parts[7]
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return restaurants
         
         
         def load_menus():
             menus = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'menu.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         item_id = parts[0]
                         menus[item_id] = {
                             'item_id': parts[0],
                             'restaurant_id': parts[1],
                             'item_name': parts[2],
                             'category': parts[3],
                             'description': parts[4],
                             'price': parts[5],
                             'availability': parts[6]
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return menus
         
         
         def load_cart():
             cart = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'cart.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         cart_id = parts[0]
                         cart[cart_id] = {
                             'cart_id': parts[0],
                             'item_id': parts[1],
                             'restaurant_id': parts[2],
                             'quantity': parts[3],
                             'added_date': parts[4]
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return cart
         
         
         def load_orders():
             orders = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'order.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) < 8:
                             continue
                         # delivery_address may contain commas so join from 6 to len-2 and phone_number last
                         order_id = parts[0]
                         customer_name = parts[1]
                         restaurant_id = parts[2]
                         order_date = parts[3]
                         total_amount = parts[4]
                         status = parts[5]
                         # Delivery address may contain commas, join all parts till second last
                         # phone number last
                         # Because design spec shows example lines with embedded commas
                         delivery_address = ','.join(parts[6:-1])
                         phone_number = parts[-1]
         
                         orders[order_id] = {
                             'order_id': order_id,
                             'customer_name': customer_name,
                             'restaurant_id': restaurant_id,
                             'order_date': order_date,
                             'total_amount': total_amount,
                             'status': int(status),
                             'delivery_address': delivery_address,
                             'phone_number': phone_number
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return orders
         
         
         def load_order_items():
             order_items = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'order_items.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         order_item_id = parts[0]
                         order_id = parts[1]
                         item_id = parts[2]
                         quantity = parts[3]
                         price = parts[4]
         
                         if order_id not in order_items:
                             order_items[order_id] = []
                         order_items[order_id].append({
                             'order_item_id': order_item_id,
                             'item_id': item_id,
                             'quantity': quantity,
                             'price': price
                         })
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return order_items
         
         
         def load_deliveries():
             deliveries = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'delivery.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         delivery_id = parts[0]
                         order_id = parts[1]
                         driver_name = parts[2]
                         driver_phone = parts[3]
                         vehicle_info = parts[4]
                         status = parts[5]
                         estimated_time = parts[6]
         
                         deliveries[order_id] = {
                             'delivery_id': delivery_id,
                             'driver_name': driver_name,
                             'driver_phone': driver_phone,
                             'vehicle_info': vehicle_info,
                             'status': status,
                             'estimated_time': estimated_time
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return deliveries
         
         
         def load_reviews():
             reviews = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'review.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) < 6:
                             continue
                         review_id = parts[0]
                         restaurant_id = parts[1]
                         customer_name = parts[2]
                         rating = parts[3]
                         review_text = ','.join(parts[4:-1])
                         review_date = parts[-1]
         
                         if restaurant_id not in reviews:
                             reviews[restaurant_id] = []
                         reviews[restaurant_id].append({
                             'review_id': review_id,
                             'customer_name': customer_name,
                             'rating': rating,
                             'review_text': review_text,
                             'review_date': review_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return reviews
         
         
         # Route Implementations
         
         # Root redirect route
         @app.route('/', methods=['POST'])
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         # Dashboard route
         @app.route('/dashboard', methods=['POST'])
         def dashboard():
             restaurants = load_restaurants()
         
             # Feature: pick few featured restaurants (top 3 by rating)
             try:
                 featured_restaurants = sorted(restaurants.values(), key=lambda x: float(x['rating']), reverse=True)[:3]
             except ValueError:
                 featured_restaurants = list(restaurants.values())[:3]
         
             # Pick popular cuisine - we can find the cuisine that appears most
             cuisine_count = {}
             for r in restaurants.values():
                 cuisine_count[r['cuisine']] = cuisine_count.get(r['cuisine'], 0) + 1
             popular_cuisine = None
             if cuisine_count:
                 popular_cuisine = max(cuisine_count, key=cuisine_count.get)
             else:
                 popular_cuisine = ''
         
             return render_template('dashboard.htm', featured_restaurants=featured_restaurants, popular_cuisine=popular_cuisine)
         
         
         # Browse restaurants route
         @app.route('/restaurants', methods=['POST'])
         def browse_restaurants():
             restaurants = load_restaurants()
             restaurants_list = list(restaurants.values())
         
             # Extract cuisines dictionary
             cuisines = {}
             for r in restaurants_list:
                 if r['cuisine'] not in cuisines:
                     cuisines[r['cuisine']] = []
                 cuisines[r['cuisine']].append(r)
         
             # get search query list from form
             search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '')
             search_terms = [term.strip().lower() for term in search_query.split()] if search_query else []
         
             # Filter restaurants by search terms if any
             if search_terms:
                 filtered_restaurants = []
                 for r in restaurants_list:
                     combined = (r['name'] + ' ' + r['cuisine'] + ' ' + r['address']).lower()
                     if all(term in combined for term in search_terms):
                         filtered_restaurants.append(r)
             else:
                 filtered_restaurants = restaurants_list
         
             return render_template('restaurants.html', restaurants=filtered_restaurants, cuisines=cuisines, search_query=search_terms)
         
         
         # Restaurant menu route
         @app.route('/menu/<int:restaurant_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def restaurant_menu(restaurant_id):
             restaurants = load_restaurants()
             menus = load_menus()
         
             restaurant = next((r for r in restaurants.values() if int(r['restaurant_id']) == restaurant_id), None)
             if not restaurant:
                 return "Restaurant not found", 404
         
             # Filter menu items belonging to this restaurant and available
             menu_items = [m for m in menus.values() if m['restaurant_id'] == str(restaurant_id) and m['availability'] == '1']
         
             # For specification: menu_item dictionary - unclear usage. We provide first menu item or empty dict if none
             menu_item = menu_items[0] if menu_items else {}
         
             return render_template('menu.html', restaurant=restaurant, menu_item=menu_item, restaurant_id=restaurant_id)
         
         
         # Item details route
         @app.route('/item/<int:item_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def item_details(item_id):
             menus = load_menus()
         
             item = next((m for m in menus.values() if int(m['item_id']) == item_id), None)
             if not item:
                 return "Item not found", 404
         
             return render_template('item_detail.html', item=item, item=item_id)
         
         
         # Shopping cart route
         @app.route('/cart', methods=['GET'])
         def shopping_cart():
             cart = load_cart()
             menus = load_menus()
         
             # Build cart_items dictionary keyed by item_id with quantity and price info
             cart_items = {}
             total_amount = 0.0
         
             for c in cart.values():
                 item_id = c['item_id']
                 quantity_str = c['quantity']
                 try:
                     quantity = int(quantity_str)
                 except ValueError:
                     quantity = 0
         
                 item = menus.get(item_id)
                 if not item:
                     continue
         
                 try:
                     price = float(item['price'])
                 except ValueError:
                     price = 0.0
         
                 total_item_price = price * quantity
         
                 cart_items[item_id] = {
                     'item': item,
                     'quantity': quantity,
                     'total_price': total_item_price
                 }
                 total_amount += total_item_price
         
             total_amount = round(total_amount, 2)
             return render_template('cart.htm', cart_items=cart_items, total_amount=total_amount)
         
         
         # Checkout route
         @app.route('/checkout', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def checkout():
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Receive delivery info
                 customer_name = request.form.get('customer_name', '')
                 delivery_address = request.form.get('delivery_address', '')
                 phone_number = request.form.get('phone_number', '')
                 payment_method = request.form.get('payment_method', '')
                 delivery_info = [customer_name, delivery_address, phone_number, payment_method]
                 return render_template('checkout.html', delivery_info=delivery_info)
             else:
                 # GET - show cart items
                 cart = load_cart()
                 menus = load_menus()
         
                 cart_items = {}
                 for c in cart.values():
                     item_id = c['item_id']
                     quantity_str = c['quantity']
                     try:
                         quantity = int(quantity_str)
                     except ValueError:
                         quantity = 0
         
                     item = menus.get(item_id)
                     if not item:
                         continue
         
                     cart_items[item_id] = {
                         'item': item,
                         'quantity': quantity
                     }
                 return render_template('checkout.html', cart_items=cart_items)
         
         
         # Active orders route
         @app.route('/orders/active', methods=['POST'])
         def active_orders():
             orders = load_orders()
             status_filter_str = request.form.get('status_filter', '0')
             try:
                 status_filter = int(status_filter_str)
             except ValueError:
                 status_filter = 0
         
             filtered_orders = {}
             if status_filter == 0:
                 filtered_orders = orders
             else:
                 for oid, o in orders.items():
                     if o['status'] == status_filter:
                         filtered_orders[oid] = o
         
             return render_template('active_orders.html', active_orders=filtered_orders, status_filter=status_filter)
         
         
         # Order tracking route
         @app.route('/orders/track/<int:order_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def order_tracking(order_id):
             orders = load_orders()
             deliveries = load_deliveries()
             order_items = load_order_items()
             menus = load_menus()
         
             order = next((o for o in orders.values() if int(o['order_id']) == order_id), None)
             if not order:
                 return "Order not found", 404
         
             delivery_driver = deliveries.get(str(order_id), [])
             # Order items dict with item detail
             items_in_order = order_items.get(str(order_id), [])
         
             # Build dict keyed by item_id with item details and quantity
             detailed_order_items = {}
             for i in items_in_order:
                 item_id = i['item_id']
                 quantity = i['quantity']
                 item_detail = menus.get(item_id, None)
                 if item_detail:
                     detailed_order_items[item_id] = {
                         'item': item_detail,
                         'quantity': quantity,
                         'price': i['price']
                     }
         
             return render_template('track_order.html', order=order, delivery_driver=delivery_driver, order_items=detailed_order_items, order=order_id)
         
         
         # Reviews route
         @app.route('/reviews', methods=['POST'])
         def reviews():
             reviews_data = load_reviews()
             filter_rating_str = request.form.get('filter_rating', '0')
             try:
                 filter_rating = int(filter_rating_str)
             except ValueError:
                 filter_rating = 0
         
             filtered_reviews = {}
             if filter_rating == 0:
                 filtered_reviews = reviews_data
             else:
                 for rid, revs in reviews_data.items():
                     filtered_list = [r for r in revs if int(r['rating']) == filter_rating]
                     if filtered_list:
                         filtered_reviews[rid] = filtered_list
         
             return render_template('reviews_html', reviews=filtered_reviews, filter_rating=filter_rating)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Helper functions to load data from respective files
         
         def load_restaurants():
             restaurants = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'restaurant.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         restaurant_id = parts[0]
                         restaurants[restaurant_id] = {
                             'restaurant_id': restaurant_id,
                             'name': parts[1],
                             'cuisine': parts[2],
                             'address': parts[3],
                             'phone': parts[4],
                             'rating': parts[5],
                             'delivery_time': parts[6],
                             'min_order': parts[7]
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return restaurants
         
         
         def load_menus():
             menus = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'menu.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         item_id = parts[0]
                         menus[item_id] = {
                             'item_id': item_id,
                             'restaurant_id': parts[1],
                             'item_name': parts[2],
                             'category': parts[3],
                             'description': parts[4],
                             'price': parts[5],
                             'availability': parts[6]
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return menus
         
         
         def load_cart():
             cart = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'cart.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         cart_id = parts[0]
                         cart[cart_id] = {
                             'cart_id': cart_id,
                             'item_id': parts[1],
                             'restaurant_id': parts[2],
                             'quantity': parts[3],
                             'added_date': parts[4]
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return cart
         
         
         def load_orders():
             orders = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'order.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         # Some fields may contain commas, adjust by joining address components
                         if len(parts) < 8:
                             continue
                         order_id = parts[0]
                         customer_name = parts[1]
                         restaurant_id = parts[2]
                         order_date = parts[3]
                         total_amount = parts[4]
                         status = parts[5]
                         # Join delivery address parts from index 6 up to the last but one
                         delivery_address = ','.join(parts[6:-1])
                         phone_number = parts[-1]
                         try:
                             status_int = int(status)
                         except ValueError:
                             status_int = 0
                         orders[order_id] = {
                             'order_id': order_id,
                             'customer_name': customer_name,
                             'restaurant_id': restaurant_id,
                             'order_date': order_date,
                             'total_amount': total_amount,
                             'status': status_int,
                             'delivery_address': delivery_address,
                             'phone_number': phone_number
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return orders
         
         
         def load_order_items():
             order_items = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'order_items.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         order_item_id = parts[0]
                         order_id = parts[1]
                         item_id = parts[2]
                         quantity = parts[3]
                         price = parts[4]
         
                         if order_id not in order_items:
                             order_items[order_id] = []
                         order_items[order_id].append({
                             'order_item_id': order_item_id,
                             'item_id': item_id,
                             'quantity': quantity,
                             'price': price
                         })
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return order_items
         
         
         def load_deliveries():
             deliveries = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'delivery.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         delivery_id = parts[0]
                         order_id = parts[1]
                         driver_name = parts[2]
                         driver_phone = parts[3]
                         vehicle_info = parts[4]
                         status = parts[5]
                         estimated_time = parts[6]
         
                         deliveries[order_id] = {
                             'delivery_id': delivery_id,
                             'driver_name': driver_name,
                             'driver_phone': driver_phone,
                             'vehicle_info': vehicle_info,
                             'status': status,
                             'estimated_time': estimated_time
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return deliveries
         
         
         def load_reviews():
             reviews = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'review.txt')
             try:
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) < 6:
                             continue
                         review_id = parts[0]
                         restaurant_id = parts[1]
                         customer_name = parts[2]
                         rating = parts[3]
                         review_text = ','.join(parts[4:-1])
                         review_date = parts[-1]
         
                         if restaurant_id not in reviews:
                             reviews[restaurant_id] = []
                         reviews[restaurant_id].append({
                             'review_id': review_id,
                             'customer_name': customer_name,
                             'rating': rating,
                             'review_text': review_text,
                             'review_date': review_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return reviews
         
         
         # Route implementations per specification
         
         # Route: / (root_redirect), POST, redirect to /dashboard
         @app.route('/', methods=['POST'])
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         # Route: /dashboard, POST, template: dashboard.htm
         @app.route('/dashboard', methods=['POST'])
         def dashboard():
             restaurants = load_restaurants()
             # Featured restaurants: top 3 by rating
             try:
                 featured_restaurants = sorted(restaurants.values(), key=lambda r: float(r['rating']), reverse=True)[:3]
             except Exception:
                 featured_restaurants = list(restaurants.values())[:3]
         
             # Popular cuisine (most frequent cuisine)
             cuisine_counts = {}
             for r in restaurants.values():
                 cuisine_counts[r['cuisine']] = cuisine_counts.get(r['cuisine'], 0) + 1
             popular_cuisine = ''
             if cuisine_counts:
                 popular_cuisine = max(cuisine_counts, key=cuisine_counts.get)
         
             return render_template('dashboard.htm', featured_restaurants=featured_restaurants, popular_cuisine=popular_cuisine)
         
         
         # Route: /restaurants, POST, template: restaurants.html
         @app.route('/restaurants', methods=['POST'])
         def browse_restaurants():
             restaurants = load_restaurants()
             cuisines = {}
             for r in restaurants.values():
                 if r['cuisine'] not in cuisines:
                     cuisines[r['cuisine']] = []
                 cuisines[r['cuisine']].append(r)
         
             search_query_raw = request.form.get('search_query', '')
             search_query = [term.strip().lower() for term in search_query_raw.split()] if search_query_raw else []
         
             filtered_restaurants = []
             if search_query:
                 for r in restaurants.values():
                     combined_text = (r['name'] + ' ' + r['cuisine'] + ' ' + r['address']).lower()
                     if all(term in combined_text for term in search_query):
                         filtered_restaurants.append(r)
             else:
                 filtered_restaurants = list(restaurants.values())
         
             return render_template('restaurants.html', restaurants=filtered_restaurants, cuisines=cuisines, search_query=search_query)
         
         
         # Route: /menu/<int:restaurant_id>, POST, template: menu.html
         @app.route('/menu/<int:restaurant_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def restaurant_menu(restaurant_id):
             restaurants = load_restaurants()
             menus = load_menus()
         
             restaurant = next((r for r in restaurants.values() if int(r['restaurant_id']) == restaurant_id), None)
             if not restaurant:
                 return "Restaurant not found", 404
         
             menu_items = [m for m in menus.values() if m['restaurant_id'] == str(restaurant_id) and m['availability'] == '1']
         
             menu_item = menu_items[0] if menu_items else {}
         
             # In context variable names as per spec: restaurant (list) and menu_item (dict)
             return render_template('menu.html', restaurant=restaurant, menu_item=menu_item, restaurant_id=restaurant_id)
         
         
         # Route: /item/<int:item_id>, POST, template: item_detail.html
         @app.route('/item/<int:item_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def item_details(item_id):
             menus = load_menus()
         
             item = next((m for m in menus.values() if int(m['item_id']) == item_id), None)
             if not item:
                 return "Item not found", 404
         
             return render_template('item_detail.html', item=item, item=item_id)
         
         
         # Route: /cart, GET, template: cart.htm
         @app.route('/cart', methods=['GET'])
         def shopping_cart():
             cart = load_cart()
             menus = load_menus()
         
             cart_items = {}
             total_amount = 0.0
         
             for c in cart.values():
                 item_id = c['item_id']
                 quantity = 0
                 try:
                     quantity = int(c['quantity'])
                 except:
                     quantity = 0
         
                 item = menus.get(item_id)
                 if not item:
                     continue
         
                 try:
                     price = float(item['price'])
                 except:
                     price = 0.0
         
                 total_price = price * quantity
         
                 cart_items[item_id] = {
                     'item': item,
                     'quantity': quantity,
                     'total_price': total_price
                 }
         
                 total_amount += total_price
         
             total_amount = int(total_amount)  # as int per spec
         
             return render_template('cart.htm', cart_items=cart_items, total_amount=total_amount)
         
         
         # Route: /checkout, POST and GET, template: checkout.html
         @app.route('/checkout', methods=['POST', 'GET'])
         def checkout():
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 delivery_info = []
                 try:
                     customer_name = request.form.get('customer_name', '')
                     delivery_address = request.form.get('delivery_address', '')
                     phone_number = request.form.get('phone_number', '')
                     payment_method = request.form.get('payment_method', '')
                     delivery_info = [customer_name, delivery_address, phone_number, payment_method]
                 except Exception:
                     delivery_info = []
                 return render_template('checkout.html', delivery_info=delivery_info)
             else:
                 # GET
                 cart = load_cart()
                 menus = load_menus()
                 cart_items = {}
                 for c in cart.values():
                     item_id = c['item_id']
                     quantity = 0
                     try:
                         quantity = int(c['quantity'])
                     except:
                         quantity = 0
         
                     item = menus.get(item_id)
                     if not item:
                         continue
         
                     cart_items[item_id] = {
                         'item': item,
                         'quantity': quantity
                     }
                 return render_template('checkout.html', cart_items=cart_items)
         
         
         # Route: /orders/active, POST, template: active_orders.html
         @app.route('/orders/active', methods=['POST'])
         def active_orders():
             orders = load_orders()
             status_filter_str = request.form.get('status_filter', '0')
             try:
                 status_filter = int(status_filter_str)
             except:
                 status_filter = 0
         
             if status_filter == 0:
                 filtered_orders = orders
             else:
                 filtered_orders = {oid: o for oid, o in orders.items() if o['status'] == status_filter}
         
             return render_template('active_orders.html', active_orders=filtered_orders, status_filter=status_filter)
         
         
         # Route: /orders/track/<int:order_id>, POST, template: track_order.html
         @app.route('/orders/track/<int:order_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def order_tracking(order_id):
             orders = load_orders()
             deliveries = load_deliveries()
             order_items = load_order_items()
             menus = load_menus()
         
             order = next((o for o in orders.values() if int(o['order_id']) == order_id), None)
             if not order:
                 return "Order not found", 404
         
             delivery_driver = deliveries.get(str(order_id), [])
             items_for_order = order_items.get(str(order_id), [])
         
             detailed_order_items = {}
             for item in items_for_order:
                 item_id = item['item_id']
                 quantity = item['quantity']
                 price = item['price']
                 item_detail = menus.get(item_id)
                 if item_detail:
                     detailed_order_items[item_id] = {
                         'item': item_detail,
                         'quantity': quantity,
                         'price': price
                     }
         
             return render_template('track_order.html', order=order, delivery_driver=delivery_driver, order_items=detailed_order_items, order=order_id)
         
         
         # Route: /reviews, POST, template: reviews_html
         @app.route('/reviews', methods=['POST'])
         def reviews():
             all_reviews = load_reviews()
             filter_rating_str = request.form.get('filter_rating', '0')
             try:
                 filter_rating = int(filter_rating_str)
             except:
                 filter_rating = 0
         
             if filter_rating == 0:
                 filtered_reviews = all_reviews
             else:
                 filtered_reviews = {}
                 for rid, rev_list in all_reviews.items():
                     filtered_list = [rev for rev in rev_list if int(rev['rating']) == filter_rating]
                     if filtered_list:
                         filtered_reviews[rid] = filtered_list
         
             return render_template('reviews_html', reviews=filtered_reviews, filter_rating=filter_rating)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)
